  <script>
   function alleyGetParameterByName(name) { 
                var testName = name.replace(/[\[\]]/g, '\\$&'); 
                var regex = new RegExp('[?&]' + testName + '(=([^]*)|&|#|$)'), 
                    results = regex.exec(window.location.href); 
                if (!results) return null; 
                if (!results[2]) return null; 
                return decodeURIComponent(results[2].replace(/\+/g, ' ')); 
            }
            var abCohort = alleyGetParameterByName('ab-cohort');
            if (abCohort) { 
                googletag.cmd.push(function(){
                    googletag.pubads().setTargeting('abCohort', abCohort);
                });
            }
  </script>

  <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jquery-color/2.1.2/jquery.color.min.js">

  <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/Chart.js/2.3.0/Chart.min.js">

  <script>
   $(document).ready(function() {
             charts = $('.chart');
        
             // https://stackoverflow.com/questions/1152024/best-way-to-generate-a-random-color-in-javascript/14187677#14187677
             function rainbow() {
               // 30 random hues with step of 12 degrees
               var hue = Math.floor(Math.random() * 30) * 12;
        
               return $.Color({
                 hue: hue,
                 saturation: 0.9,
                 lightness: 0.6,
                 alpha: 1
               }).toHexString();
             };
            
             // https://stackoverflow.com/questions/25880767/chart-js-number-format
             window.addCommas = function (nStr) {
               nStr += '';
               x = nStr.split('.');
               x1 = x[0];
               x2 = x.length > 1 ? '.' + x[1] : '';
               var rgx = /(\d+)(\d{3})/;
               while (rgx.test(x1)) {
                   x1 = x1.replace(rgx, '$1' + ',' + '$2');
               }
               return x1 + x2;
             }
        
             function initCharts() {
               charts.each(function() {
                 $(this).attr('data-bar-color',rainbow());
                 var frame = $('<div class="frame">').appendTo($(this));
                 $('<canvas>').appendTo(frame);
               });
             }
        
             function drawCharts(commasFun) {
               charts.each(function(commasFun) {
                 var raceID = $(this).attr('data-race-id');
                 var backgroundColor = $(this).attr('data-bar-color');
                 var frame = $(this).find('.frame');
                 var ctx = $(this).find('canvas');
                 var urlParams = {c: 'result', m: 'view', race_id: raceID};
                 var maintainAspectRatio = true;
                 var cb = new Date().getTime();
                 var url = '/app/election-results/index.php?cb=' + cb + '&' + $.param(urlParams);
                 
                 if (raceID == '54338' && window.innerWidth <= 425) {
                   frame.css('height', '420px');
                   maintainAspectRatio = false;
                 }
        
                 $.ajax({method: 'GET', url: url}).done(function (race) {
                   var labels = [];
                   var voteTotals = [];
                   for (var i = 0; i < race.choices.length; i++) {
                     var choice = race.choices[i];
                     var percentage = choice.vote_percentage;
                     labels.push(choice.description + ': ' + percentage + '%');
                     voteTotals.push(choice.vote_total);
                   }
        
                   Chart.defaults.global.defaultFontColor = '#222';
                   Chart.defaults.global.barThickness = 111;
                   Chart.defaults.global.barPercentage	 = 0.2;
        
                   var chart = new Chart(ctx, {
                     type: 'horizontalBar',
                     data: {
                       'labels': labels,
                       'datasets': [{
                         label: 'Votes',
                         data: voteTotals,
                         backgroundColor: backgroundColor
                       }]
                     },
                     options: {
                       title: {
                         display: true,
                         text: race.title
                       },
                       legend: {
                         display: false
                       },
                       scales: {
                         xAxes: [{
                           ticks: {
                             beginAtZero: true,
                             display: false
                           },
                           scaleLabel: {
                            display: true,
                            labelString: race.num_precincts_reporting + ' of ' + race.num_precincts_expected + ' precincts reporing'
                           }
                         }],
                         yAxes: [{
                           categoryPercentage: 1.0
                         }]
                       },
                       tooltips: {
                         callbacks: {
                           label: function(tooltipItem, data) {
                             return 'Votes: ' + window.addCommas(tooltipItem.xLabel);
                           }
                         }
                       },
                       maintainAspectRatio: maintainAspectRatio
                     }
                   });
                 });
               });
             }
        
             window.redrawIntervalID = window.setInterval(drawCharts, 60000);
             initCharts();
             drawCharts();
           });
  </script>

                     <div class="card-headline">
                      <h2 class="tnt-headline">
                       <a class="tnt-asset-link" href="/baton_rouge/sports/lsu/article_f1a2f456-8a85-11eb-ba87-836a8c5bad88.html">
                        F. King Alexander again facing potential firing, discipline in Oregon over LSU allegations
                       </a>
                      </h2>
                     </div>
                     <div class="card-lead">
                      <p class="tnt-summary">
                       Less than a week after placing F. King Alexander on 10 weeks of probation, the Oregon State University Board of Trustees plans to meet again Tuesday and could potentially consider further discipline against the former LSU president.
                       <a class="tnt-asset-link read-more-link" href="/baton_rouge/sports/lsu/article_f1a2f456-8a85-11eb-ba87-836a8c5bad88.html">

                        </a>

                    <div class="card-body">
                     <div class="card-labels">
                      <div class="card-label-section text-muted">
                       <a class="tnt-section-tag" href="/baton_rouge/sports/lsu">
                        LSU
                       </a>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div class="card-headline">
                      <h2 class="tnt-headline">
                       <a class="tnt-asset-link" href="/baton_rouge/sports/lsu/article_f002d642-8a90-11eb-9071-3797e3da6795.html">
                        LSU bounces back to beat Mississippi State, avoid weekend sweep
                       </a>
                      </h2>
                     </div>
                     <div class="card-lead">
                      <p class="tnt-summary">
                       After losing the first two games of the weekend series, No. 10 LSU avoided getting swept for the first time since April 2018 by beating No. 6 Mississippi State 8-3, a much-needed bounce back after getting shut out for the first time this season.
                       <a class="tnt-asset-link read-more-link" href="/baton_rouge/sports/lsu/article_f002d642-8a90-11eb-9071-3797e3da6795.html">
                        Read the full story
                       </a>
                      </p>
                     </div>

      <script>
       (function() {
          $(document).ready(function() {  
            var container = $('#masthead-col-one');
            var stickyNote = $('#ad-477840, #ad-478791, #ad-478790, #ad-504703, #ad-504714, #ad-504722, #ad-519714, #ad-529275');
            var closeButton = $('<div>').text('');
         
            function closeStickyNote() {
              stickyNote.fadeOut();
            }
            
            window.setTimeout(closeStickyNote, 12000);
            
            stickyNote.prependTo(container);
            stickyNote.css({
              'background': '#fff',
              'position': 'absolute',
              'z-index': 9999,
              'left': 250,
              'top': 20,
              'box-shadow': '5px 5px 10px rgba(0,0,0,0.45)',
              'transform': 'rotate(-5deg)',
              '-webkit-transform': 'rotate(-5deg)',
            });
            
            closeButton.appendTo(stickyNote);
            closeButton.css({
              'position': 'absolute',
              'z-index': 9999,
              'left': -5,
              'bottom': -5,
              'width': 20,
              'height': 20,
              'background': '#111',
              'color': '#fff',
              'border': '2px solid #fff',
              'border-radius': 20,
              'font-size': 18,
              'font-weight': 'bold',
              'text-align': 'center',
              'line-height': '17px',
              'cursor': 'pointer',
            });
            closeButton.on('click', closeStickyNote);
          })
        })();
      </script>

            if (typeof __tnt.advertisements == 'undefined') {
                __tnt.compatibility.status = 'FAIL: object 0 undefined';
                return false;
            }
            return true;
        };
        __tnt.compatibility.notification = function() {

                    var el = document.createElement('div');

                    document.querySelector('#asset-content .asset-body').appendChild(el);
                }

                                message.parentNode.removeChild(message);
                            } else {
                                message.style.display = 'block';
                                }
                        }, 100);
                    }
                );
            };
        (function() {
            function compatibilityCheck() {
                if (!__tnt.compatibility.check()) {
                    __tnt.trackEvent({
                        'category':'subscription',
                        'action':'adblock',
                        'label':'adblock detected',
                        'value':'1'
                    });
                    }

            } else {
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', compatibilityCheck);
            }
        })();

  <script>
   __tnt.trackEvent = function(obj) {
            if (typeof obj === 'object') {
                    if (obj.category && obj.action) {
                        __tnt.googleEvent(obj);
                    } else if (obj.network && obj.socialAction) {
                        __tnt.googleSocial(obj);
                    } else if (obj.url) {
                        __tnt.googlePageView(obj);
                    }
                    if (typeof TNCMS.Tracking != 'undefined' && obj.metric) {
                        TNCMS.Tracking.addEvent({
                            app: obj.app,
                            metric: obj.metric,
                            id: obj.uuid
                        });
                    }
            }
        };

        if (__tnt.trackEventLater.length > 0) {
            __tnt.trackEventLater.forEach(function(obj) {
                __tnt.trackEvent(obj);
            });
        }

        Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('body [data-track]')).forEach(function(el) {
            el.addEventListener(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function() {
                __tnt.trackEvent(JSON.parse(el.dataset.track));
            });
        });
        Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('body [data-tncms-track-event]')).forEach(function(el) {
            el.addEventListener(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function() {
                __tnt.trackEvent(JSON.parse(el.dataset.tncmsTrackEvent));
            });
        });
        
        Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('body [data-tncms-track-dmp]')).forEach(function(el) {
            el.addEventListener(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function() {
                var dmpData = el.dataset.tncmsTrackDmp;
                
            });
        });
  </script>

  <script>
   /*<![CDATA[*/ 
                __tnt.googleEvent = function(obj) {
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.trigger',
                             'tncms.event.trigger.category': obj.category,
                             'tncms.event.trigger.action': obj.action,
                             'tncms.event.trigger.label': obj.label, 
                             'tncms.event.trigger.value': obj.value
                    });
                }
                /* Virtual page view */
                __tnt.googlePageView = function(obj) {
                    var sURL = obj.url.replace(/^.*\/\/[^\/]+/, '');
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.virtual_pageview',
                            'tncms.event.virtual_pageview.url': sURL,
                            'tncms.event.virtual_pageview.title': obj.title
                    });
                }
                /* Social event */
                __tnt.googleSocial = function(obj) {
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.social',
                            'tncms.event.social.network': obj.network,
                            'tncms.event.social.action': obj.socialAction,
                            'tncms.event.social.target': obj.url
                    });
                } /*]]>*/
  </script>
